Column densities were derived through a homogeneous rotation-diagram approach, with CH$_3$CN used as a proxy excitation-temperature reference when needed. In CH$_3$OH-normalized abundance-ratio space, CH$_3$OCHO/CH$_3$OH and CH$_3$OCH$_3$/CH$_3$OH show the strongest pairwise correlation, whereas the correlations involving CH$_3$CHO are weaker. No clear monotonic trends are found with Galactocentric distance or beam-averaged H$_2$ column density. Comparison with previous observations places the CH$_3$OCHO--CH$_3$OCH$_3$ behavior within the range of earlier abundance-ratio measurements, while CH$_3$CHO shows larger inter-study variation. A representative warm-up chemical model is used only for qualitative comparison with the observed abundance ranges, which are most closely matched during the decline from the post-desorption abundance peaks in the model. These results provide homogeneous beam-averaged abundance-ratio constraints for common O-bearing COMs in high-mass star-forming regions and show that their source-to-source behavior is molecule-dependent rather than fully described by a single common abundance pattern.

### [115] [Predicting the unpredictable: binary--single scattering with machine learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16763)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: binary-single encounters 是常见的恒星系统相互作用，属于非可积混沌三体问题，用N体模拟计算代价高昂，因此需要一个快速、准确且物理可解释的替代模型。

Method: 使用物理启发的特征，在数值积分生成的平衡类别数据集上训练XGBoost多分类器，并通过特征重要性分析和basin-entropy分析探究预测失败原因。

Result: 模型测试准确率为88.32%，top-2准确率为98.77%；二元系统硬度是主导预测因子；误分类集中在交换与分层结果之间的混沌边界附近。

Abstract: Binary--single encounters occur frequently in stellar systems, constitute a non-integrable chaotic three-body problem, and are computationally expensive when treated with N-body codes. We aim to construct an accurate and physically interpretable surrogate model for binary--single scattering final states (ionization, flyby, exchange, or hierarchical), evaluate the reliability of its probabilistic predictions, and trace its predictive failures to the underlying chaotic nature of the scattering problem. We trained an XGBoost multiclass classifier on a class-balanced dataset of numerically integrated binary--single scattering experiments, using physically motivated features. The model achieves a test accuracy of 88.32 percent and a top-2 accuracy of 98.77 percent. Feature importance indicates binary hardness as the dominant predictor. Misclassifications concentrate near the chaotic boundary separating exchange and hierarchical outcomes. Basin-entropy analysis reveals that such misclassifications are due to intrinsically ambiguous regions of parameter space. Therefore, a fast machine-learning surrogate can predict binary--single scattering final states with high accuracy, and residual errors arise from chaotic regions rather than model inadequacy.

### [116] [Machine learning prediction of binary formation in three-body gravitational encounters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16776)
*Ahmad Farhani Asl*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于XGBoost的机器学习模型，用于从三体初始条件快速、准确且可解释地预测双星形成，性能优异（各项指标均>0.94），推理速度比直接N体积分快约400倍，关键物理参数为质量层级和硬度比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三体相遇频繁、混沌且计算昂贵，难以在大规模模拟中高效预测是否形成双星，亟需一种准确、可解释、高效的替代方法。

Method: 使用REBOUND+IAS15生成三体散射数据集，构建含30个物理特征的XGBoost二分类器，并进行特征重要性分析与概率校准评估。

Result: 模型在平衡测试集上准确率、精确率、召回率、F1分数均超0.94，ROC-AUC和PR-AUC达0.99；特征重要性显示质量层级和硬度比主导结果；预测概率校准良好（ECE=0.02）；推理速度快400倍；在不同作用半径下泛化良好，但在弱相互作用区性能下降。

Abstract: Three-body encounters are frequent events in stellar systems, intrinsically chaotic, and computationally costly to model with direct N-body integration. Predicting whether such encounters lead to binary formation is therefore challenging, particularly in large-scale simulations. We aim to develop an accurate and physically interpretable machine-learning model that predicts binary formation from the initial conditions of three-body encounters, to assess its reliability, and to identify the physical parameters that most strongly determine the outcome. We trained an XGBoost binary classifier on a balanced dataset of three-body scattering experiments computed with the REBOUND code and the IAS15 integrator. The input to the model consists of 30 physically motivated features describing the masses, energies, and kinematics of the initial configuration. The classifier achieves excellent performance on a balanced test set, with accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score all above 0.94, and with ROC-AUC and PR-AUC values of 0.99. Feature-importance analysis shows that the outcome is governed primarily by the mass hierarchy and hardness ratio of the encounter, followed by velocity fraction and mass entropy. The predicted probabilities are well calibrated, with an expected calibration error (ECE) of 0.02. Inference is approximately 400 times faster than direct N-body integration. The model also generalizes well across encounter radii, although its performance decreases in the weak-interaction regime where binary formation becomes intrinsically rare. These results show that machine learning can provide fast, accurate, and physically interpretable predictions of binary formation in three-body encounters. Such models offer a practical complement to direct N-body simulations and may enable efficient probability estimates in large-scale simulations of stellar systems.

### [117] [Temporal Correlations Between Fuzzy Dark Matter and Baryonic Matter in Virialized Core-Halo Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16917)
*Ivan Alvarez-Rios,Francisco S. Guzman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用FDM波性导致的干涉颗粒结构产生的时变引力场，探索其是否能引起可观测的重子物质动力学效应。

Method: 采用三维Schrödinger-Poisson-Euler系统数值模拟FDM-气体耦合演化；FDM由多并合初态弛豫至核-晕结构，气体建模为理想气体；在动力学平衡后分析两组分的时间涨落、相关函数及谱特征。

Result: FDM密度场呈现显著高频涨落，而气体形成更平滑、寿命更长的相干结构；尽管气体受FDM引力势影响，但其动力学与FDM干涉涨落之间缺乏强时间相关性，该结论在所考察的气体温度范围内均成立。

Conclusion: 重子物质主要响应FDM晕的整体引力势，而非其相位依赖的颗粒细节；这种弱时间耦合可能限制通过局域重子时间涨落直接探测FDM颗粒结构的可行性。

Abstract: Fuzzy Dark Matter (FDM) predicts the existence of virialized halos with interference-driven granular structure generated by the wave nature of ultralight bosons. Since these fluctuations produce time-dependent gravitational fields, they can be proposed as a potential source of observable dynamical effects on baryonic matter. In this work we test whether such fluctuations generate measurable temporal correlations between FDM and a coupled gas component. We evolve coupled FDM-gas configurations with the Schrödinger-Poisson-Euler system in three dimensions. The FDM component is initialized through multimerger configurations that relax toward core-halo structures, while the baryonic component is modeled as an ideal gas. After virialization, we analyze the temporal fluctuations of both components through correlation functions and spectral diagnostics. The FDM density field shows fluctuations with significant high-frequency content, whereas the gas develops smoother and longer-lived coherent structures. Although the gas dynamically responds to the gravitational potential generated by the FDM halo, we find no strong temporal correlation between the interference-driven fluctuations of FDM and the gas dynamics. This behavior persists across the explored range of gas temperatures. Our results indicate that baryonic matter reacts to the global gravitational potential of the virialized halo rather than to the detailed phase-dependent granular structure of FDM. This weak temporal coupling may limit the possibility of directly detecting FDM granularity through local baryonic temporal fluctuations.

### [118] [Disentangling the Morphology of Palomar~5: Effects of the Bar, Spiral Arms, LMC, and Halo Flattening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17040)
*Zhenghao He,Long Wang,Zi-yi Zhou,Yang Huang,Eugene Vasiliev*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过包含多种银河系结构（如旋臂、棒、晕扁率、大麦哲伦云及棒减速）的碰撞性直接N体模拟，研究了球状星团Palomar 5过去30亿年的演化及其潮汐尾特征，发现银河晕形状、棒和LMC对流迹形态有显著但差异化的效应，但现有模型无法同时复现所有观测特征，表明需更精确的初始条件与更复杂的银河势模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Palomar 5及其潮汐尾是对银河系时变引力势高度敏感的探针，可用于检验星团演化与银河系结构模型。

Method: 采用PeTar代码进行碰撞性直接N体模拟，纳入含旋臂、棒、晕扁率、大麦哲伦云（LMC）及棒减速的银河势模型，回溯Pal~5过去3 Gyr演化。

Result: 银河晕扁率主导投影流迹走向；LMC主要影响近心点距离与星团质量演化；银河棒显著调控流迹长度与物质再分布，导致密度结构与前后尾不对称；当前模型无法同时匹配Erkal et al. (2017)与Xiao et al. (2025)的多项观测（星团演化、流迹长度/轨迹/宽度/线密度剖面）。

Conclusion: Pal~5流迹的精细建模需更准确的初始星团参数与更复杂的银河势（如暗物质子晕、巨分子云等小尺度扰动），未来可结合自洽N体模拟与粒子喷射法提升效率。

Abstract: The Palomar~5 (Pal~5) globular cluster and its tidal tails provide a sensitive probe of globular-cluster evolution in the time-dependent Milky Way potential. We study the past 3~Gyr evolution of Pal~5 using collisional direct \(N\)-body simulations with \texttt{PeTar}, adopting Galactic potential models that include spiral arms, the Galactic bar, halo flattening, the Large Magellanic Cloud (LMC), and bar deceleration. We find that halo shape strongly influences the projected stream track, reflecting Pal~5's sensitivity to Galactic force-field flattening. The LMC causes only modest direct changes to the present-day projected stream morphology, but can alter the pericentric distance and hence the progenitor's mass evolution. The Galactic bar strongly affects stream length and debris redistribution along the tails, producing model-dependent density structures and leading--trailing asymmetries. Comparison with observations from Erkal et al. (2017) and Xiao et al. (2025) shows that no single model simultaneously reproduces all observed properties of Pal~5, including cluster evolution, stream length, track, width, and line-density profile. Although our simulations capture several global properties, the remaining discrepancies indicate that a more precise match likely requires better constraints on the initial properties of the Pal~5 progenitor and a more complex Galactic potential, including perturbations from small-scale perturbers such as dark matter subhalos and giant molecular clouds. Future work may combine self-consistent direct \(N\)-body simulations with particle-spray methods to investigate these discrepancies more efficiently.

</details>


### [119] [Super-Jeans Fragmentation and Supply-Limited Accretion: Environment-Dependent Co-Evolution of Low- and High-Mass Cores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17215)
*Dan Miao,Guang-Xing Li,Patricio Sanhueza*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过分析ASHES项目中39个大质量红外暗云团块内的839个原恒星核，发现最重的三个核的质量占总核质量的比例（约25%、16%、10%）在质量增长序列中保持恒定，表明高质核的种子很早就确立了质量主导地位；同时Gini系数上升说明低质量核在后期才逐渐形成；提出一种环境依赖的碎裂图像：中心种子在高密度湍流核中通过输运驱动的超Jeans碎裂快速形成高质核，并在供料受限下同步生长，而外围低质核则因密度较低、缺乏非稳态流入加速而在包层中较晚、以Jeans式碎裂方式持续产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大质量恒星诞生过程中原恒星核的形成与增长机制是关键科学问题。

Method: 基于ASHES项目观测数据，对39个大质量红外暗云团块中839个分辨至数千天文单位尺度的原恒星核进行质量统计分析，结合Gini系数量化质量分布不均匀性，并构建环境依赖的碎裂与吸积物理图像。

Result: 发现最重三核质量占比恒定（~25%、16%、10%），Gini系数随质量增长序列上升；揭示中心高质核早期确立主导地位，外围低质核延迟形成；提出‘输运驱动超Jeans碎裂+供料受限同步生长’模型。

Conclusion: 大质量恒星区核群的协同演化由非稳态密度调控碎裂与供料受限吸积共同驱动，小尺度核增长与大尺度气体库调控无缝衔接，局地自由落体时间是主导因素。

Abstract: Protostellar core formation and growth in high-mass star-forming regions remain key to understanding massive star birth. We analyze the masses of 839 cores (resolved at scales of a few thousand au) from the ASHES project targeting 39 massive infrared dark cloud clumps. The masses of the three most massive cores scale linearly with the total core mass. They maintain a constant mass fraction of ~25%, 16%, and 10% along the mass growth sequence. These fractions reveal that the progenitor seeds destined to become high-mass cores establish their mass dominance very early. Additionally, the Gini coefficient (a statistical measure of inequality) of the core mass distributions increases along the mass growth sequence, confirming that the relative population of low-mass cores builds up toward later stages. This points to an environment-dependent fragmentation picture: central prestellar seeds rapidly evolve into high-mass cores via transport-driven super-Jeans fragmentation under rapid, non-stationary mass accumulation in high-density, turbulent hubs, subsequently maintain their dominance through supply-limited synchronized growth (at R<1 pc, n_H2>10^5 cm^-3), while the formation of the surrounding low-mass cores is relatively delayed due to their lower gas densities and the lack of non-stationary inflow acceleration effect, resulting in their continuous emergence through Jeans-like fragmentation in lower-density envelopes. This picture is consistent with a gravity-driven scenario where the local free-fall time is the controlling factor. Our analysis suggests that non-stationary density-regulated fragmentation and supply-limited accretion jointly drive the synchronized co-evolution of the core cluster, seamlessly linking small-scale core growth with large-scale reservoir regulation.

</details>


### [120] [Revealing a multi-zone circumnuclear dust response in UGC~11487 through phase-resolved WISE W1--W2 diagnostics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17815)
*I. O. Izviekova,O. V. Kompaniiets,I. B. Vavilova*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过对MIR选源TDE候选体UGC 11487/WTP14adeqka长达十年的WISE/NEOWISE观测进行相位分辨分析，结合多波段数据建模，揭示其尘埃回响具有延迟、宽化、冷却及色度滞后等特征，支持其为被遮蔽的TDE，并证实WISE相位分辨诊断可有效探测亚秒差距尺度的尘埃响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用相位分辨的WISE/NEOWISE W1-W2光变分析，结合计时、颜色与流量诊断、现象学建模、基于流体力学的团块状尘埃回响计算，以及孔径匹配的紫外至射电能谱分布。

Result: 发现十年尺度MIR耀发具有约224±45天延迟（对应0.188±0.038 pc）、W2响应更宽、色度滞后、温度由~900 K冷却至500–600 K；红外光度峰值达~3×10⁴³ erg s⁻¹，总能量(2.9–3.8)×10⁵¹ erg；单成分模型被强烈排除（ΔBIC=281.7），优选双成分现象学模型；流体-团块模拟可复现观测特征。

Conclusion: UGC 11487/WTP14adeqka是一个被结构化核周尘埃再处理的遮蔽型TDE类暂现源；WISE相位分辨诊断可有效恢复遮蔽吸积核暂现源中亚秒差距尺度的尘埃响应特征。

Abstract: Mid-infrared (MIR) flares provide a direct probe of dust reprocessing in obscured tidal disruption event (TDE) candidates when the primary optical or ultraviolet flare is weak, missed, or strongly attenuated. We present a phase-resolved analysis of the WISE/NEOWISE W1-W2 evolution of the MIR-selected TDE candidate UGC 11487/WTP14adeqka over 2014-2024. We combine timing, colour, and flux diagnostics with phenomenological modelling, hydrodynamically motivated clumpy dust-echo calculations, and an aperture-matched ultraviolet-to-radio spectral energy distribution of the host. The decade-long flare shows a delayed and broader W2 response, colour hysteresis, and cooling from approximately 900 K to 500-600 K. Positive-fluence centroids yield a preferred delay of $224 +/- 45$ d, corresponding to $0.188 +/- 0.038$ pc. The effective infrared luminosity peaks at approximately $3 x 10^{43}$ erg s$^{-1}$, and the integrated infrared energy is $(2.9-3.8) x 10^{51}$ erg. A single self-similar MIR response is strongly disfavoured, with Delta BIC = 281.7, while the preferred compact description is a two-component phenomenological model. Representative hydro-clumpy calculations reproduce the empirical diagnostics in a structured, multi-zone dust-response scenario. The host is a moderately star-forming isolated barred disc without a dominant persistent active galactic nucleus component. These results support an obscured TDE-like accretion transient reprocessed by structured circumnuclear dust and show that phase-resolved WISE diagnostics can recover characteristic sub-parsec response scales in obscured accretion-powered nuclear transients.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present results from spectroscopic observations of three interacting galaxy systems, each associated with a primary galaxy - VCC 1748, SDSS J1106, and 2MASX J0834 - which have been proposed as potential examples of reverse morphological transformation from elliptical to spiral types driven by external gas accretion. Using Gemini/GMOS longslit spectroscopy, we obtain spectra along longslits connecting the regions of interest between the two galaxies in each pair. We model the spatially binned spectra with the Penalized Pixel-Fitting (pPXF) method to derive velocity fields and radial profiles of gas-phase metallicity, stellar metallicity, and stellar population age. Among the three systems, only the VCC 1748 system provides spectra with sufficiently high signal-to-noise ratios (S/N) to reveal coherent velocity and metallicity structures extending between the companion spiral galaxy and its elliptical target. The velocity profile along the gas-bridge of the system is smooth and continuous from the companion spiral arm to the target galaxy, and the elliptical target, VCC 1748, exhibits younger stellar populations and a high star formation rate (SFR) in its newly formed disk regions compared to its central parts. These findings indicate in-situ star formation at the newly-formed spiral arm of the elliptical target, consistent with ongoing gas inflow from the spiral companion into the elliptical target. Altogether, the results capture an intermediate stage of morphological evolution in which an originally quiescent elliptical galaxy begins to assemble a rotationally supported disk through interaction-driven gas accretion.

### [123] [The initial conditions and initial mass functions of Alpha Persei, Pleiades and Praesepe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17300)
*L. Hobart,H. Baumgardt,S. Sweet*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用Gaia DR3数据结合N体模拟、机器学习与MCMC方法，重构了Alpha Persei、Pleiades和Praesepe三个疏散星团的初始质量函数（IMF）及结构参数，发现IMF呈三段分段幂律分布，存在星团间高质端斜率的显著弥散，支持IMF非普适性及环境依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验初始质量函数（IMF）是否具有普适性，及其是否依赖于星团环境；同时需准确扣除动力学演化与未分辨双星的影响，以可靠反演初始状态。

Method: 基于Gaia DR3天体测量与测光数据识别星团成员，并融合UKIDSS和HIPPARCOS近红外/光学数据；采用贝叶斯框架下的蒙特卡洛模拟校正未分辨双星；结合N体模拟、机器学习代理模型与MCMC算法反演初始结构参数（如初始恒星数、双星分数、半质量半径、IMF）。

Result: 得到三段分段幂律IMF：低、中、高质量端转折质量分别为0.24–0.50和0.91–1.20太阳质量，中质量端平均斜率α_med=1.72±0.09，高质量端α_high=2.98±0.22；高质量端斜率在星团间存在显著弥散（σ_high=0.29±0.16），而中质量端无显著变化（σ_med=0.00±0.14）；双星分数为20–24%。

Conclusion: 结果支持IMF并非完全普适，呈现‘偏轻’（相比Salpeter形式）且随环境（星团）变化的特征，对IMF的形成机制及其与恒星形成环境的关系提供了关键观测约束。

Abstract: We have determined the initial mass function (IMF) and structural properties of the open clusters Alpha Persei, Pleiades and Praesepe using Gaia DR3 astrometry and photometry. Cluster members were identified using primarily Gaia astrometry, supplemented with near-infrared UKIDSS and optical HIPPARCOS survey data with stellar masses down to $0.10-0.17$ MSun. We measure and correct for unresolved binaries in each cluster using photometry and Monte Carlo simulations in a Bayesian framework, finding present-day fractions between ($20.0\pm0.8$)% and ($23.8\pm1.2$)%. Through a novel approach that combines N-body simulations with machine learning emulators and MCMC algorithms, we have also determined the most probable initial number of stars, binary fraction, half-mass radius and mass function under the assumption that early gas removal does not significantly influence the subsequent cluster evolution. We find a best-fitting initial mass function described by a three-stage broken power-law distribution with break masses in the ranges $0.24-0.50$ MSun and $0.91-1.20$ MSun and average slopes of $α_{\rm med}=1.72\pm0.09$ and $α_{\rm high}=2.98\pm0.22$. While the low-mass slope remains sensitive to the adopted mass-luminosity relation, this IMF reproduces the present-day clusters well once their dynamical evolution is taken into account. We find evidence of scatter in the high mass IMF between the individual clusters, as described by the measured dispersions in mass function slopes of $σ_{\rm high}=0.29\pm0.16$, whereas the intermediate mass slope shows no significant variation with $σ_{\rm med}=0.00\pm0.14$. Our findings provide additional evidence for a (compared to a Salpeter MF) top-light IMF and a cluster-to-cluster variation of the IMF. They therefore provide constraints on the universality of the IMF and its dependence on environmental conditions.

### [124] [A Rest-frame K-band View of Bulge Growth in Massive Dusty Star-forming Galaxies at z~2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17424)
*Ken-ichi Tadaki*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用JWST和ALMA观测研究z~2处16个大质量尘埃遮蔽星暴星系的核球形成过程，发现多数星系中恒星质量分布与尘埃辐射同样致密，核球已基本形成；部分星系则仍处于核球致密化阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高红移大质量星系中核球如何在尘埃遮蔽环境下快速形成并演化。

Method: 结合JWST MIRI F770W（探查静止K波段恒星质量分布）、NIRCam多波段及ALMA 870 μm（示踪尘埃辐射）成像数据，进行径向剖面分析、光度剖面分解（bulge+disk）及CIGALE SED拟合。

Result: F770W有效半径与870 μm一致（中位比0.95），显著小于F444W；堆叠分析显示bulge-to-total比为0.50；消光Av由中心2.6 mag降至外围1.5 mag，sSFR剖面平坦；两个星系中870 μm比F770W致密3–6倍，表明其仍处于核球致密化阶段。

Abstract: We study bulge formation in 16 massive dusty star-forming galaxies at z~2 by combining JWST MIRI F770W imaging, NIRCam imaging in eight bands, and ALMA 870 um data. At the median redshift of z=2.18, the F770W band probes the rest-frame 2.4 um light, close to the rest-frame K band, and traces the stellar mass distribution with little effect from dust attenuation. The effective radii measured in F770W agree with those of the 870 um dust emission, with a median ratio of 0.95, and are typically 23% smaller than those in F444W. The rest-frame K-band imaging is therefore essential to measure the true extent of the stellar mass, which is as compact as the dusty star-forming regions. In stacks of the 16 galaxies at a matched resolution, the 870 um and F770W profiles agree closely out to 8 kpc, and a bulge plus disk decomposition of the F770W stack gives a bulge-to-total ratio of 0.50. Fitting the SEDs in radial bins with CIGALE, we find that the attenuation decreases from Av=2.6 mag at the center to 1.5 mag at $r\gtrsim7$ kpc, while the specific star formation rate profile is flat. In these galaxies the bulge is already in place, and the whole system grows toward compact quiescent galaxies within about 1 Gyr. In two galaxies, by contrast, the 870 um emission is 3 to 6 times more compact than the F770W light, which suggests that they are still in the bulge-building compaction phase. Our sample may thus catch massive galaxies in several phases of bulge formation.

### [125] [Anomalously high deuterium fractionation in a galactic translucent cloud: a challenge to chemical models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17529)
*Gan Luo,Zhi-Yu Zhang,Thomas G. Bisbas,Di Li,Serena Viti,Roberto Neri,Junzhi Wang,Siyi Feng,Ningyu Tang,Daniel R. Rybarczyk,Lingrui Lin*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文报告了在透光云中首次探测到DCN和DNC，发现其氘化丰度远高于预期，挑战了现有化学模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氘化物种（D-物种）长期以来被用作诊断冷密分子云物理条件和化学演化的工具，但在弥散和透光云中的观测仍然稀少。

Method: 利用IRAM NOEMA望远镜对一个透光云（A_V = 1.2±0.2 mag, n_H2 = 3.9±0.2×10^2 cm^-3）进行高灵敏度吸收观测，探测DCN和DNC。

Result: 首次在透光云中探测到DCN和DNC，DCN/HCN和DNC/HNC丰度比分别为3.3±0.6×10^-3和3.6±1.2×10^-3，比[D]/[H]元素丰度（1.5×10^-5）高出两个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 观测结果显著偏离现有考虑氘化 fractionation 的化学模型，暗示透光云中存在未知的氘化增强机制，可能与弥散致密核或致密云消散形成的动态演化结构有关。

Abstract: Deuterated (D-) species have long been proposed to diagnose the physical conditions and chemical evolution of cold dense molecular clouds. While deuterium fractionation has been extensively measured in dense cores, observations in diffuse and translucent clouds remain rare. We report here the detection of DCN and DNC toward a translucent cloud ($A_{\rm V} =1.2\pm0.2$ mag, $n_{\rm H_2}$ = $3.9\pm0.2\times10^2$ cm$^{-3}$) through sensitive absorption observations with the IRAM NOrthern Extended Millimeter Array (NOEMA). This detection reaches the lowest column-density and volume-density regime in which deuteration has been observed so far. Interestingly, the observed DCN/HCN and DNC/HNC abundance ratios ($3.3\pm0.6\times10^{-3}$ and $3.6\pm1.2\times10^{-3}$, respectively), which are more than two orders of magnitude higher than the element abundance [D]/[H] (1.5$\times$10$^{-5}$), suggest an unexpected enhancement of deuterium fractionation in the translucent cloud. These results represent a significant departure from established chemical models considering deuterium fractionation, which predict negligible formation of D-molecules in such environments. Although it remains unclear how D-molecules built up their abundances in translucent gas, a dispersed dense core scenario could potentially explain the observed high deuterium fraction. This interpretation is consistent with the idea proposed by Price et al. (2003) more than two decades ago: a translucent cloud may be a transient, dynamically evolving structure formed through the dissipation of a dense molecular cloud.

### [126] [The Intrinsic Multiphase Gas--Black Hole Connection across Scales in IllustrisTNG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17567)
*Xiaoxia Zhang,Taotao Fang,Shulan Yan,Si-Yue Yu,Feng Yuan*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用IllustrisTNG100模拟研究了超大质量黑洞与星系周围多相介质之间的关系，发现黑洞质量与冷气体质量在扣除恒星和暗物质晕质量影响后呈显著负相关，支持AGN反馈逐步清除冷气体的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解超大质量黑洞与多相星系周介质（CGM）的关系对揭示星系与其中心黑洞共同演化至关重要。

Method: 基于IllustrisTNG100模拟中z=0的5089个中心星系样本，测量黑洞质量与不同温度区间（冷、凉、温、热）气体质量在多个半径范围内的偏相关性，并控制恒星质量和暗物质晕质量等混杂因素。

Result: 黑洞质量与R200及0.15R200内冷气体质量呈显著负偏相关（ρ≈−0.37），而与温、热气体无明显内在关联；残差分析显示过质量黑洞星系系统性缺乏冷气体，且该反相关在不同环境密度与星系类型中均存在。

Conclusion: 结果定量支持AGN反馈通过逐步耗尽冷气体调控星系演化，为多波段观测提供了可检验的预测。

Abstract: The relationship between supermassive black holes and the multiphase circumgalactic medium is central to understanding the co-evolution of galaxies and their central black holes. We investigate this relationship using the IllustrisTNG100 simulation with a sample of 5089 central galaxies at $z=0$, measuring the partial correlation between central black hole mass and the mass of cold ($T < 10^4$K), cool ($10^4 \le T < 10^5$K), warm ($10^5 \le T < 10^6$K), and hot ($T \ge 10^6$K) gas within $0.03R_{200}$, $0.15R_{200}$, and $R_{200}$, after accounting for stellar and dark matter halo mass. We find that after removing these confounding factors, black hole mass shows a significant negative partial correlation ($ρ\approx -0.37$) with cold gas within $R_{200}$ and $0.15R_{200}$, whereas warm and hot gas exhibit no substantial intrinsic correlation. The residual plane reveals a threshold pattern: galaxies with over-massive black holes show systematically reduced cold gas, consistent with the cumulative impact of AGN feedback. The anti-correlation persists across environments with a weak trend in local density, and varies with galaxy type (star-forming, green valley, and quenched). These results provide a quantitative multiphase diagnostic of AGN feedback in TNG and support a picture in which feedback progressively removes cold gas, offering testable predictions for future multiwavelength surveys.

### [127] [On the Separation Between the Brightest Cluster Galaxy and the Intracluster Light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17616)
*Emanuele Contini,Sukyoung K. Yi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于模型的框架，通过平衡BCG外溢恒星质量和ICL内含质量，确定最优孔径半径以最小化ICL质量恢复偏差；该半径在物理单位下随晕质量幂律增长，在Rvir单位下近乎与质量无关，且在z=0–2范围内稳定，显著提升了BCG和ICL质量的恢复精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为建立观测中BCG-ICL测量与理论模型内在组分之间的可靠联系，需定义一个物理上有依据的孔径分离方案，以减少因孔径选择不当导致的质量估计偏差。

Method: 基于半解析模型FEGA25预测的BCG和ICL本征成分，对每个暗晕确定使ICL质量恢复偏差最小的最优孔径半径，其核心是权衡孔径外BCG恒星质量与孔径内ICL质量。

Result: 在z=0时，最优物理孔径r_cut ∝ M_halo^0.28；以R_vir归一化后，r_cut/R_vir ≈ 0.045（在10^14 M⊙处），且该比值在z=0–2间稳定；BCG质量恢复误差<8%（最低分位），ICL质量恢复中位数≈1，平均散射±3%。

Conclusion: 所提出的孔径定义具有物理基础、质量与红移稳健性，为弥合BCG-ICL观测与模拟之间差距提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: We present a model-based framework to define an aperture separation between the brightest cluster galaxy (BCG) and the intracluster light (ICL). Using the intrinsic BCG and ICL components predicted by the semi-analytic model \texttt{FEGA25}, we determine, for each halo, the aperture radius that minimizes the bias in the recovered ICL mass. The optimal radius is obtained by balancing the BCG stellar mass lying outside the aperture with the ICL mass enclosed within it. At $z=0$, the optimal aperture in physical units increases with halo mass approximately as $r_{\rm cut}\propto M_{\rm halo}^{0.28}$, close to the expected virial scaling. When expressed in units of the virial radius, the aperture becomes nearly independent of halo mass, with $r_{\rm cut}/R_{\rm vir}\simeq 0.045$ at $10^{14}M_\odot$. Applying the resulting aperture prescriptions, we recover the intrinsic BCG mass to better than 8\% (lowest percentile), while the ICL mass is recovered with median values very close to unity, and an average scatter of $\pm 3\%$. Extending the analysis to $z=1$ and $z=2$, we find that the mass trends remain similar, with the slope and intercept of $r_{\rm cut}/R_{\rm vir}$ that stay stable. Robustness tests show that the inferred aperture is most sensitive to the ICL concentration and BCG size, but the main trends are preserved. Our results provide a physically motivated aperture definition for connecting observational BCG--ICL measurements to intrinsic model components.

### [128] [Feature-driven anomaly flagging in obscured active galactic nucleus light curves with autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17728)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该方法在所研究AGN样本中识别出11.18%为异常；针对遮蔽型AGN，找到一组精简特征子集，性能与全特征集相当；SHAP分析揭示了模型判别异常的关键特征及其物理意义。

Abstract: Active galactic nuclei (AGN) are among the most complex classes of astrophysical objects, displaying a wide range of variability and observational properties. Identifying unusual AGN is crucial for understanding the physical mechanisms behind their emission better and for discovering potentially new subclasses or rare behaviors. With the increasing volume of data from next-generation surveys, machine-learning-based anomaly detection offers a promising approach to flagging and investigating such outliers systematically. We explore the use of unsupervised algorithms with a feature-driven approach to flag anomalous AGN, further explored by a human expert. The main focus is on obscured AGN, which tend to be harder to characterize. The algorithm we used was an AutoEncoder, which we trained on features extracted from the light curves rather than working with the light curves directly. The unsupervised nature of the method allows the detection of anomalies without relying on labeled data. To properly characterize the feature space and the detection process, we used the SHAP method. Our method flagged $11.18\%$ of the AGN we studied as anomalous. We focused in particular on anomalous obscured AGN and identified a refined subset of features that yields a comparable performance to the full set. Together with an in-depth analysis of the anomalies, this provides insight into how the AutoEncoder assigns anomalous status and which features are most indicative of astrophysically interesting behaviors or phenomena.

### [129] [Two Peas in a Pod: The First Confirmed Dual Active Galactic Nucleus within a Green Pea Galaxy System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17729)
*Konstantinos Kouroumpatzakis,Peter G. Boorman,Jiří Svoboda,Ryan Pfeifle,Abhijeet Borkar,Maitrayee Gupta,Daniel Stern,Andreas Zezas*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文报告了在Green Pea星系SDSS J162209.41+352107.5中首次确认的双活动星系核（AGN），揭示了低质量致密星系中多个超大质量黑洞可同时高效增长，为研究早期宇宙星系与黑洞协同演化提供了邻近实验室。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙中致密、剧烈恒星形成的星系主导星系增长，但其中超大质量黑洞（SMBH）的增长仍缺乏约束；Green Pea星系作为其近邻类似体，其SMBH增长机制尚不明确，尤其缺乏多黑洞同时吸积的直接观测证据。

Method: 利用Chandra X射线望远镜成像分辨出投影距离8.4 kpc的两个硬X射线源，并通过Keck望远镜光谱观测确认二者具有共同红移及独立的宽巴尔末发射线和高电离AGN谱线。

Result: 首次在Green Pea星系中确认存在双AGN，且该系统为低质量、致密、非典型并合星系，不同于以往多数在大质量并合系统中发现的双AGN。

Abstract: The growth of galaxies in the early Universe is thought to be dominated by compact, intensely star-forming systems, yet the corresponding growth of supermassive black holes (SMBHs) within such environments remains poorly constrained. Green Pea galaxies are nearby analogs of rapidly assembling galaxies in the early Universe owing to their compact morphologies, intense star formation, low metallicities, and extreme ionization conditions. Although galaxy interactions are thought to trigger episodes of rapid SMBH growth, direct observations of simultaneous accretion onto multiple SMBHs in compact, intensely star-forming galaxies are lacking. Here we report the discovery of the first confirmed dual active galactic nucleus (AGN) in a Green Pea system, SDSS J162209.41+352107.5. Chandra imaging resolves two luminous hard X-ray sources separated by 8.4 kpc in projection, demonstrating simultaneous accretion onto two SMBHs. Follow-up Keck spectroscopy confirms that the two optical nuclei share a common redshift and independently exhibit broad Balmer emission and high-ionization AGN emission lines. Unlike most known dual AGN, which are typically found in massive mergers, J162209.41+352107.5 is a compact low-mass system analogous to galaxies thought to dominate early phases of galaxy assembly. These findings demonstrate that efficient growth of multiple SMBHs can occur in such environments and establish Green Pea galaxies as nearby laboratories for investigating the interplay between galaxy interactions, star formation, and black-hole growth under conditions analogous to those prevalent in the young Universe.

### [130] [Far-Infrared Star Formation Rates of Quasar Host Galaxies from Multiwavelength Spectral Energy Distribution Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17752)
*Xiaotong Feng,Xue-Bing Wu,Yuming Fu,Yuxuan Pang,Rui Zhu,Huimei Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过多波段光谱能量分布（SED）分解，研究了202个SDSS和PG类星体在红移0.02–0.8范围内的远红外（FIR）恒星形成率（SFR）及其宿主星系性质，评估了不同SED拟合工具（CIGALE与AGNfitter）及冷尘埃模板带来的系统误差，并探讨了SFR、AGN吸积效率、尘埃辐射场强度等物理量之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠地测定类星体宿主星系的恒星形成率（SFR）对理解黑洞增长与星系演化协同关系至关重要；而远红外波段是测量被尘埃遮蔽恒星形成的最佳窗口，但其SFR估计受AGN污染和模型选择影响显著，亟需系统性评估。

Method: 利用从光学至远红外（含JCMT/SCUBA-2 450/850 μm）的多波段测光数据，采用CIGALE和AGNfitter两种SED拟合代码，并结合多种冷尘埃模板，对202个类星体进行SFR_FIR建模与不确定性量化；同时分析SFR与主序偏离度、Eddington比、红外辐射锥光度比（L_tor/L_Edd）、尘埃辐射场强度U_min及WISE波段指标的相关性。

Result: 五种FIR SFR估计间的中位模型依赖弥散为0.14 dex；AGNfitter结果比CIGALE平均低0.09 dex；SCUBA-2数据对多数源SFR修正仅~0.01 dex，但在Herschel覆盖不足或射电噪源中影响显著；多数宿主星系位于或高于恒星形成主序；MS偏离度与直接Eddington比无明显相关，但与红外L_tor/L_Edd正相关；U_min随总光度和尘埃温度升高而增大；WISE W2+W3联合Herschel可经验性指示AGN贡献分数f_AGN。

Conclusion: FIR SFR估计具有可观的模型依赖系统误差，需谨慎选用SED拟合方法与模板；类星体宿主星系普遍存在活跃恒星形成，其SFR与AGN活动参数存在非平凡关联（如依赖红外选示的吸积效率而非直接Eddington比），提示黑洞与星系共演化机制可能受尘埃辐射物理调控；多波段（尤其WISE+Herschel）可提供实用的AGN主导性诊断指标。

Abstract: Reliable star formation rates (SFRs) are essential for studying the connection between black hole growth and quasar host galaxies. We study the far-infrared (FIR) SFRs and the host galaxy properties of 202 SDSS and PG quasars at $0.02<z\lesssim0.8$, spanning $\log({\rm SFR}_{\rm FIR}/M_\odot\,{\rm yr}^{-1})\simeq-0.45$--$2.76$, using multiwavelength spectral energy distribution (SED) decomposition. The photometry covers wavelengths from the optical to the FIR and is supplemented by JCMT/SCUBA-2 observations at 450 and 850 $μ$m. We model the SEDs with CIGALE and AGNfitter and adopt multiple cold dust templates to quantify systematic uncertainties. The median model-dependent scatter among the five FIR SFR estimates is $0.14$ dex, and AGNfitter gives FIR SFRs lower than the mean CIGALE estimate by a median of $0.09$ dex. For the 58 quasars with SCUBA-2 coverage, including SCUBA-2 data changes the adopted FIR SFR by only $\sim$0.01 dex on average but can affect individual sources with limited Herschel coverage or radio-loud emission. Within our FIR-constrained sample, many quasar hosts lie on or above the star-forming main sequence, but the redshift-dependent FIR selection of the SDSS subsample limits conclusions about the full quasar-host population. We find no clear correlation between the main-sequence (MS) offset and the direct Eddington ratio, while the offset is positively related to the infrared-based $L_{\rm tor}/L_{\rm Edd}$ proxy. The minimum radiation field intensity in the dust model, $U_{\rm min}$, increases with bolometric luminosity and dust temperature. WISE W2 (4.6 $μ$m) and W3 (12 $μ$m) combined with Herschel bands can also provide useful empirical indicators of $f_{\rm AGN}$.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于Osipkov-Merritt分布函数并结合Lynden-Bell daemon协议引入净角动量的初始平衡态，开展一系列无碰撞N体模拟，并分析密度与相空间模式增长、轴比及三轴性指数。

Result: 发现内部旋转在Fridman-Polyachenko-Shukhman指数接近一致性临界值的径向各向异性模型中可削弱径向轨道不稳定性强度，但在近稳定模型中略微促进其发生；即使存在中心密度尖峰，仍可形成不稳定内棒结构。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between radial velocity anisotropy and internal rotation in self-gravitating systems characterised by initial spherical symmetry and a moderate density cusp. We study the stability properties of such configurations to disentangle the impact of anisotropy, rotation, and density structure on the formation of triaxial stellar systems.
  We perform a set of collisionless $N$-body simulations starting from initial equilibria with a phase space distribution function of the class introduced by Osipkov and Merritt, modified to impose a net global angular momentum with the Lynden-Bell daemon protocol. We analyse the growth of the density and phase space distribution modes, as well as the axial ratios and triaxiality index of the final configurations. We find that internal rotation has a mitigating effect on the strength of the radial orbit instability in radially anisotropic models with Fridman-Polyachenko-Shukhman index close to its value for consistency, while it slightly enhances the onset of the instability in nearly stable models. From the analysis of the growth rate of the density modes, we also find that an inner bar, though unstable for maximally rotating initial conditions, is formed even in systems with initial profiles with a central density cusp.

In Arp~105N, strong nebular emission lines and large equivalent widths $EW(Hα)=77.6\pm1.3$ $\overset{\circ}{\mathrm {A}}$ and $EW(Hβ)=15.8\pm1.7$ $\overset{\circ}{\mathrm {A}}$ imply a dominant starburst age of $\sim$6 - 10~Myr under an instantaneous-burst assumption, while the FUV emission suggests star formation sustained over the past $\sim100 - 200$~Myr. The relatively high metallicity, $\sim2/3,Z_\odot$ (based on the strong-line method), is consistent with expectations for a tidal dwarf galaxy formed from material inherited from the host galaxy. Together, these results suggest that Arp~105N hosts a composite stellar population, consisting of older stars stripped from the host galaxy and younger stars formed in situ. ### [133] [Testing [O II] $\lambda3727$ as a Star Formation Rate Tracer in Quasar Host Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17788)
*Xiaotong Feng,Xue-Bing Wu,Yuming Fu,Yuxuan Pang,Rui Zhu,Huimei Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估[O II] λ3727发射线在I型类星体中作为星形成率（SFR）示踪器的可靠性，因其易受尘埃消光、金属丰度和AGN窄线区（NLR）污染影响。

Method: 基于202个SDSS和PG类星体样本，通过光谱拟合测量[O II]、[O III]和窄巴耳末线；结合多波段SED分解获得参考远红外（FIR）SFR；对[O II] SFR进行消光和金属丰度校正，并分别在扣除/不扣除AGN贡献（基于[O III]估计）下与FIR SFR比较。

Result: 扣除AGN贡献后，[O II]与FIR SFR中位偏移为−0.20±0.72 dex（全样本）和−0.17±0.69 dex（信噪比>5子样本）；未扣除时偏移为0.00±0.69 dex和0.12±0.66 dex。

Conclusion: [O II]可作为类星体宿主星系统计SFR的有用示踪器，但单个天体仍需仔细处理AGN污染、消光、金属丰度、孔径效应及红移相关系统误差。

Abstract: The [O II] $\lambda3727$ emission line is a widely used star formation rate (SFR) tracer. However, its application to type I quasars is not straightforward, because the line can be affected by dust extinction, metallicity and contamination from the AGN narrow-line region (NLR). We test the reliability of [O II] SFRs using a sample of 202 SDSS and PG quasars, by comparing [O II] SFRs and reference far-infrared (FIR) SFRs derived from multiwavelength SED decomposition. We measure [O II], [O III], and narrow Balmer emission lines by spectral fitting. Then, we calculate [O II] SFRs after correcting dust extinction and metallicity. We then compare these SFRs with the FIR SFRs, both with and without subtracting the AGN contribution estimated from [O III]. After this correction, the median offset between [O II] and FIR SFRs is $-0.20\pm0.72$ dex for the full analysis sample and $-0.17\pm0.69$ dex for sources with S/N $>5$ in both [O II] and [O III]. Without subtracting the AGN contribution, the corresponding offsets are $0.00\pm0.69$ and $0.12\pm0.66$ dex. We conclude that [O II] is useful as a statistical SFR tracer for quasar host galaxies, but individual objects still require careful treatment of AGN contamination, extinction, metallicity, aperture effects, and redshift-dependent systematics.

</details>


### [134] [Spatio-kinematical structure of the Galactic Nuclear Stellar Disk revealed in VLBI astrometry of circumstellar masers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17870)
*Hiroshi Imai,Kohei Kurahara,Huib J. van Langevelde,Maria J. Rioja,Richard Dodson*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文探讨了利用SKA-VLBI天体测量技术研究银河系中心核星盘（NSD）和中央分子区（CMZ）中OH/IR恒星相关OH脉泽三维运动的可能性，旨在揭示由恒星形成活动外向传播形成的环状结构，并通过精确距离测量（三角视差或光度视差）确定该结构的主轴方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示银河系中心核星盘（NSD）中恒星形成活动外向传播所形成的环状结构，并理解其动力学与演化历史。

Method: 利用SKA-VLBI对OH脉泽（特别是1612 MHz）进行大样本、中等精度的天体测量；结合SKA-MID Band 5a（5–7 GHz）三角视差和长周期变星的周光关系获取光度视差，以获得<100 pc精度的距离信息。

Result: 预期可探测数千个OH脉泽的自行运动，呈现环状结构中的流运动特征；结合高精度距离，有望明确识别~8 kpc处可能存在的椭圆恒星环的主轴方向。

Conclusion: SKA-VLBI天体测量结合多波段距离测定，将为银河系中心恒星环结构及其形成机制提供关键观测证据。

Abstract: SKA-VLBI astrometry will enable us to measure up to thousands of three dimensional motions of OH masers associated with circumstellar envelopes (CSEs) of OH/IR stars in the Nuclear Stellar Disk (NSD) and sites of high mass star formation in the Central Molecular Zone (CMZ) of the Galactic Center (GC). It is expected that the spatio-kinematical distribution of those OH masers should indicate the existence of a ring structure in the NSD, which has formed as a result of outward propagation of star-formation activities in the GC. This is likely visualized clearly by a group of OH/IR stars, some of which should have stellar pulsation periods of >400 days and the corresponding ages of <500 Myr, and some sites of ongoing star formation. These OH/IR stars should host 1612-MHz OH masers, some of which should become targets of huge-sample VLBI astrometry, in moderate accuracy, in SKA-MID Band 2 (~1.6 GHz). The data of maser source proper motions will exhibit a stream motion in the stellar ring structure. Furthermore, the information of accurate distances (error <100 pc) of the maser sources are necessary to directly find the major-axis direction of a possible elliptical ring of stars at ~8 kpc. These distances may be yielded through trigonometric parallaxes measurable in SKA-MID Band 5a (5--7 GHz) and/or photometric parallaxes derived from the pulsation period--luminosity relation of long period variable stars hosting the maser sources.

### [135] [Ergodicity of FIRE: star formation variations within and between simulated galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18005)
*Fraser M. Smith,Robert J. Thacker*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了FIRE-2模拟星系中恒星形成的遍历性，发现单个星系偏离恒星形成主序（SFMS）的行为随时间趋于遍历，且短时标（10^7年）恒星形成率估计比长时标（10^9年）更快达到遍历行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨模拟星系中恒星形成过程是否具有遍历性，即群体统计平均是否等价于单个星系的时间平均，尤其关注其与星系偏离恒星形成主序（SFMS）的关系。

Method: 基于FIRE-2高分辨率宇宙学流体模拟，分析多个星系的恒星形成历史（SFH），比较不同SFMS定义和不同时间尺度（10^7 vs. 10^9年）的恒星形成率估计，并结合Sérsic指数表征的形态分类进行分组分析。

Result: 个体星系对SFMS的偏离随时间趋于遍历；短时标恒星形成率更快收敛至遍历行为；盘主导星系比椭球主导星系呈现更宽的SFMS偏离范围；该趋势不依赖SFMS定义或恒星形成估算方法。

Conclusion: 在当前FIRE-2模拟中，恒星形成过程在统计意义上表现出良好遍历性，但结果受限于当前样本，需进一步研究高红移演化及活动星系核（AGN）反馈的影响。

Abstract: We investigate the ergodicity of star formation in simulated galaxies from the FIRE-2 (Feedback In Realistic Environments) project. We restrict ergodicity considerations to being related to deviations from the star-forming main sequence (SFMS), and in turn whether ensemble averages across populations match time-averaged star formation histories (SFHs) based on simulated observable properties. We find that in these high-resolution simulations the deviations of individual galaxies from the SFMS tend to approach ergodic behavior over time, regardless of the SFMS definition adopted and the star formation estimator used. This trend persists when galaxy morphology, as traced by Sérsic index, is considered despite the spheroid-dominated morphologies showing a smaller range of SFMS deviations than the disk-dominated morphologies. Unsurprisingly, we find more rapid convergence to ergodic behavior for star formation estimators based on shorter time scales ($10^{7}$ years) as opposed to longer ($10^{9}$ years). We caution that these findings should be considered in the context of the current sample and that further studies, particularly of high redshift evolution and the impact of active galactic nuclei should be investigated.

</details>


### [136] [Comparing the Near-infrared Spectral Energy Distributions from Different Stellar Population Synthesis Models with SPHEREx Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18048)
*Jeong Hwan Lee,Minjin Kim,Woong-Seob Jeong,Yujin Yang,Daniel C. Masters,Kyuseok Oh,Bomee Lee,Zhaoyu Huai,Yun-Ting Cheng,Richard M. Feder,Michael Zemcov,Yongjung Kim,Dohyeong Kim,Jong-Hak Woo,Andreas L. Faisst,Howard Hui,Brendan P. Crill,Chi H. Nguyen,Asantha Cooray*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用SPHEREx近红外光谱数据，对比了四种扩展至近红外波段的恒星种群合成（SPS）模型（E-MILES、BC03、CB19、FSPS）在SDSS致密星系上的表现，发现所有模型在2.4–5 μm普遍存在0.1–0.3 mag的系统性高估，尤其在中龄星族（~1–5 Gyr）中显著；老年星族（>5 Gyr）中E-MILES在3.8–5 μm偏差较小；而发射线星系中模型因忽略非恒星辐射而在长波低估达~0.5 mag，揭示当前SPS模型在近红外需改进TP-AGB和冷星分子吸收等物理特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有恒星种群合成（SPS）模型在近红外波段性能不确定，缺乏足够观测光谱验证；SPHEREx覆盖0.7–5.0 μm的高质量谱光度数据为检验NIR SPS模型提供了理想机会。

Method: 将SPHEREx观测的SDSS致密星系（2726个无发射线星系 + 1163个发射线星系）近红外光谱，与基于SDSS光学光谱全谱拟合得到的四种NIR延伸SPS模型（E-MILES、BC03、CB19、FSPS）预测SED进行比较，分析各模型在不同年龄星族和星系类型下的偏差。

Result: 所有四种SPS模型在2.4–5 μm普遍存在0.1–0.3 mag的恒星连续谱高估，中龄星族（~1–5 Gyr）偏差最显著；老年星族（>5 Gyr）中E-MILES在3.8–5 μm偏差相对最小；发射线星系中模型因未计入非恒星辐射，在长波低估达~0.5 mag。

Conclusion: 当前SPS模型在近红外存在系统性偏差，亟需改进热脉动渐近巨星支（TP-AGB）星光及冷星分子吸收等物理成分，以提升NIR恒星谱建模精度。

Abstract: While stellar population synthesis (SPS) models have been widely used for spectral analysis in optical wavelengths, their characteristics remain uncertain in the near-infrared (NIR) due to a relative lack of observed NIR spectra. The spectrophotometric data from SPHEREx are well-suited for investigating the performance of SPS models in the NIR, thanks to its wide wavelength coverage over $0.7-5.0~{\rm μm}$. In this work, we compare the observed SPHEREx data of SDSS compact galaxies, including 2,726 non-emission-line galaxies and 1,163 emission-line galaxies, to the NIR SEDs predicted from the full spectrum fitting of SDSS optical spectra. We use four different SPS models that extend into the NIR: E-MILES, Bruzual \& Charlot (BC03), Charlot \& Bruzual (CB19), and FSPS. We find that all four models tend to overpredict the stellar continuum at $2.4-5~{\rm μm}$ by $0.1-0.3~{\rm mag}$. This trend is particularly prominent for intermediate-age stellar populations ($\sim1-5~{\rm Gyr}$), suggesting a systematic bias in the NIR SED predictions of current SPS models. For stellar populations older than $5~{\rm Gyr}$, E-MILES shows relatively smaller offsets at $3.8-5~{\rm μm}$ compared to other models. Meanwhile, for emission-line galaxies, the SPS models underestimate the SED by up to $\sim0.5~{\rm mag}$ at longer wavelengths due to the contribution of non-stellar emission. Overall, these results highlight the necessity of refining the NIR stellar spectral features in SPS models, such as emissions from thermally pulsating asymptotic giant branch stars or molecular absorptions from cool stars.

</details>


### [137] [Discovery of an Unbound Flyby Companion of UBC 63: In the Immediate Aftermath of a Close Encounter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18224)
*Samrat Biswas,Biman J Medhi,Sergio Messina,Zhanpeng Zhu,Songmei Qin,Sukanta Deb,A. H. Sheikh,H. S Das,Motohide Tamura,Maheshwar Gopinathan,Ram sagar*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用Gaia DR3数据重新研究了开放星团UBC 63，发现它并非单一星团，而是两个年龄差异显著（约541 Myr）、正在经历无束缚飞掠相互作用的双星团（UBC 63A和UBC 63B）；通过GMM分解、轨道积分与N体模拟，证实二者曾于约6 Myr前近距离相遇（~7 pc），目前正快速分离，并处于引力未束缚状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前UBC 63被归类为单一开放星团，但其物理性质存在异常；本文旨在借助高精度Gaia DR3数据，厘清其真实结构与演化状态。

Method: 在5维天体测量空间中使用高斯混合模型（GMM）进行成员识别与成分分解；结合等时线拟合估算年龄；开展轨道回溯积分与N体数值模拟以重建动力学历史；计算逃逸速度与潮汐参数评估束缚性与相互作用强度。

Result: 识别出两个统计上显著分离的子成分UBC 63A（98成员，21±4 Myr）和UBC 63B（148成员，562±43 Myr）；二者年龄差排除共形成可能；当前三维距离26±8 pc、相对速度3.60±1.80 km/s；模拟显示6 Myr前曾接近至7±2 pc，未来100 Myr内将分离至491±213 pc；系统逃逸速度远低于相对速度，确认为引力未束缚系统；观测到潮汐拉伸与超出Jacobi半径的恒星分布，支持近期强潮汐相互作用。

Conclusion: UBC 63是一个正处于飞掠阶段的未束缚双星团系统，为研究星团间短暂动力学相互作用提供了关键案例，挑战了传统单星团分类范式，并暗示其可能起源于同一巨分子云复合体。

Abstract: We re-investigate the open cluster UBC 63 using the Gaia DR3 data and show that, rather than being a single cluster as previously classified, it is a compelling candidate for a double cluster undergoing an unbound flyby interaction. A GMM decomposition performed in the 5D astrometric space reveals the two statistically distinct components, namely UBC 63A (98 members, Age = 21 $\pm$ 4 Myr) and UBC 63B (148 members, Age = 562 $\pm$ 43 Myr). A significant age difference of $Δ\mathrm{Age} = 541 \pm 43$ Myr between the clusters, rules out coeval formation. Their 3D separation of $60 \pm 29$ pc at the birth-epoch of the younger cluster, indicates that the clusters might have originated from the same molecular cloud complex. At present, the system exhibits a 3D separation of $26 \pm 8$ pc, with a relative velocity of $3.60 \pm 1.80$ km s$^{-1}$. Orbital integrations and \textit{N}-body simulations of the pair suggest that the systems had a close encounter, reaching a separation of $7 \pm 2$ pc only $\sim$~6 Myr ago and predict a rapid divergence to a separation of $491 \pm 213$ pc within the next $\sim$100 Myr. The low escape velocity ($V_{\rm esc} = 0.51 \pm 0.12$ km s$^{-1}$) of the system compared to the relative 3D velocity indicates that they are gravitationally unbound. Their low tidal factors, elongated structures and populations extending beyond the Jacobi radii may reflect a strong transient tidal interaction between the clusters.

</details>
